SAMPLE     B4C deposit with minimal purity of 98.0% enriched in   1424300100010 
           B10 to 94.0% with thickness of 14.5(8) and 15.7(8)     1424300100011 
           mu-g/cm2 and diameter of 84 mm. Two samples of each    1424300100012 
           thickness were used. B4C deposited on polished         1424300100013 
           stainless steel foil with thicknes of 0.3mm and        1424300100014 
           diameter of 100 mm                                     1424300100015 
DETECTOR   (IOCH)A twin Frisch-grid gas ionization chamber was    1424300100016 
           used. With this type of detector, a simultaneous       1424300100017 
           measurement of the energy and angular distribution     1424300100018 
           of the charged particles from the reaction is          1424300100019 
           possible in a nearly 2x2Pi geometry.The two boron      1424300100020 
           samples were mounted in a back-to-back geometry on the 1424300100021 
           common cathode of the chamber.                         1424300100022 
METHOD     (TOF) Energy of incident neutrons determined by        1424300100023 
           time-of-flight                                         1424300100024 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO)Photoneutrons produced by Bremsstrahlung in     1424300100025 
           an uranium target. Measurements were performed at      1424300100026 
           two different flight-path distances from the GELINA    1424300100027 
           neutron-producing target: L1 = 28.24 m (moderated      1424300100028 
           beam) and L2 = 57.41 m (unmoderated beam). A B4C       1424300100029 
           filter was placed in the beam, which effectively       1424300100030 
           removed neutrons with thermal and epithermal energies. 1424300100031 
CORRECTION Corrected for different sample thickness (4%) in       1424300100032 
           backside ion chamber                                   1424300100033
